18 using namespace llvm;
19 
20 // These tables are sorted by their RegOp value allowing them to be binary
21 // searched at runtime without the need for additional storage. The enum values
22 // are currently emitted in X86GenInstrInfo.inc in alphabetical order. Which
23 // makes sorting these tables a simple matter of alphabetizing the table.
24 //
25 // We also have a tablegen emitter that tries to autogenerate these tables
26 // by comparing encoding information. This can be enabled by passing
27 // X86_GEN_FOLD_TABLES=ON to cmake which fill produce X86GenFoldTables.inc
28 // in the build area. There are currently some bugs in the autogenerated table
29 // that require a manual review to copy them from the autogenerated table into
30 // this table. It is unclear if we will ever be able to fully automate this
31 // because as new instruction are added into holes in the X86 opcode map they
32 // potentially pair up with old instructions and create new entries in the
33 // tables that would be incorrect. The manual review process allows us a chance
34 // to catch these before they become observable bugs.

5514 static const X86MemoryFoldTableEntry *
5515 lookupFoldTableImpl(ArrayRef<X86MemoryFoldTableEntry> Table, unsigned RegOp) {
5516 #ifndef NDEBUG
5517  // Make sure the tables are sorted.
5518  static std::atomic<bool> FoldTablesChecked(false);
5519  if (!FoldTablesChecked.load(std::memory_order_relaxed)) {
5520  assert(std::is_sorted(std::begin(MemoryFoldTable2Addr),
5521  std::end(MemoryFoldTable2Addr)) &&
5522  std::adjacent_find(std::begin(MemoryFoldTable2Addr),
5523  std::end(MemoryFoldTable2Addr)) ==
5524  std::end(MemoryFoldTable2Addr) &&
5525  "MemoryFoldTable2Addr is not sorted and unique!");
5526  assert(std::is_sorted(std::begin(MemoryFoldTable0),
5527  std::end(MemoryFoldTable0)) &&
5528  std::adjacent_find(std::begin(MemoryFoldTable0),
5529  std::end(MemoryFoldTable0)) ==
5530  std::end(MemoryFoldTable0) &&
5531  "MemoryFoldTable0 is not sorted and unique!");
5532  assert(std::is_sorted(std::begin(MemoryFoldTable1),
5533  std::end(MemoryFoldTable1)) &&
5534  std::adjacent_find(std::begin(MemoryFoldTable1),
5535  std::end(MemoryFoldTable1)) ==
5536  std::end(MemoryFoldTable1) &&
5537  "MemoryFoldTable1 is not sorted and unique!");
5538  assert(std::is_sorted(std::begin(MemoryFoldTable2),
5539  std::end(MemoryFoldTable2)) &&
5540  std::adjacent_find(std::begin(MemoryFoldTable2),
5541  std::end(MemoryFoldTable2)) ==
5542  std::end(MemoryFoldTable2) &&
5543  "MemoryFoldTable2 is not sorted and unique!");
5544  assert(std::is_sorted(std::begin(MemoryFoldTable3),
5545  std::end(MemoryFoldTable3)) &&
5546  std::adjacent_find(std::begin(MemoryFoldTable3),
5547  std::end(MemoryFoldTable3)) ==
5548  std::end(MemoryFoldTable3) &&
5549  "MemoryFoldTable3 is not sorted and unique!");
5550  assert(std::is_sorted(std::begin(MemoryFoldTable4),
5551  std::end(MemoryFoldTable4)) &&
5552  std::adjacent_find(std::begin(MemoryFoldTable4),
5553  std::end(MemoryFoldTable4)) ==
5554  std::end(MemoryFoldTable4) &&
5555  "MemoryFoldTable4 is not sorted and unique!");
5556  assert(std::is_sorted(std::begin(BroadcastFoldTable2),
5557  std::end(BroadcastFoldTable2)) &&
5558  std::adjacent_find(std::begin(BroadcastFoldTable2),
5559  std::end(BroadcastFoldTable2)) ==
5560  std::end(BroadcastFoldTable2) &&
5561  "BroadcastFoldTable2 is not sorted and unique!");
5562  assert(std::is_sorted(std::begin(BroadcastFoldTable3),
5563  std::end(BroadcastFoldTable3)) &&
5564  std::adjacent_find(std::begin(BroadcastFoldTable3),
5565  std::end(BroadcastFoldTable3)) ==
5566  std::end(BroadcastFoldTable3) &&
5567  "BroadcastFoldTable3 is not sorted and unique!");
5568  FoldTablesChecked.store(true, std::memory_order_relaxed);
5569  }
5570 #endif
5571 
5572  const X86MemoryFoldTableEntry *Data = llvm::lower_bound(Table, RegOp);
5573  if (Data != Table.end() && Data->KeyOp == RegOp &&
5574  !(Data->Flags & TB_NO_FORWARD))
5575  return Data;
5576  return nullptr;
5577 }
5578 
5579 const X86MemoryFoldTableEntry *
5580 llvm::lookupTwoAddrFoldTable(unsigned RegOp) {
5581  return lookupFoldTableImpl(MemoryFoldTable2Addr, RegOp);
5582 }
5583 
5584 const X86MemoryFoldTableEntry *
5585 llvm::lookupFoldTable(unsigned RegOp, unsigned OpNum) {
5586  ArrayRef<X86MemoryFoldTableEntry> FoldTable;
5587  if (OpNum == 0)
5588  FoldTable = makeArrayRef(MemoryFoldTable0);
5589  else if (OpNum == 1)
5590  FoldTable = makeArrayRef(MemoryFoldTable1);
5591  else if (OpNum == 2)
5592  FoldTable = makeArrayRef(MemoryFoldTable2);
5593  else if (OpNum == 3)
5594  FoldTable = makeArrayRef(MemoryFoldTable3);
5595  else if (OpNum == 4)
5596  FoldTable = makeArrayRef(MemoryFoldTable4);
5597  else
5598  return nullptr;
5599 
5600  return lookupFoldTableImpl(FoldTable, RegOp);
5601 }
5602 
5603 namespace {
5604 
5605 // This class stores the memory unfolding tables. It is instantiated as a
5606 // ManagedStatic to lazily init the unfolding table.
5607 struct X86MemUnfoldTable {
5608  // Stores memory unfolding tables entries sorted by opcode.
5609  std::vector<X86MemoryFoldTableEntry> Table;
5610 
5611  X86MemUnfoldTable() {
5612  for (const X86MemoryFoldTableEntry &Entry : MemoryFoldTable2Addr)
5613  // Index 0, folded load and store, no alignment requirement.
5614  addTableEntry(Entry, TB_INDEX_0 | TB_FOLDED_LOAD | TB_FOLDED_STORE);
5615 
5616  for (const X86MemoryFoldTableEntry &Entry : MemoryFoldTable0)
5617  // Index 0, mix of loads and stores.
5618  addTableEntry(Entry, TB_INDEX_0);
5619 
5620  for (const X86MemoryFoldTableEntry &Entry : MemoryFoldTable1)
5621  // Index 1, folded load
5622  addTableEntry(Entry, TB_INDEX_1 | TB_FOLDED_LOAD);
5623 
5624  for (const X86MemoryFoldTableEntry &Entry : MemoryFoldTable2)
5625  // Index 2, folded load
5626  addTableEntry(Entry, TB_INDEX_2 | TB_FOLDED_LOAD);
5627 
5628  for (const X86MemoryFoldTableEntry &Entry : MemoryFoldTable3)
5629  // Index 3, folded load
5630  addTableEntry(Entry, TB_INDEX_3 | TB_FOLDED_LOAD);
5631 
5632  for (const X86MemoryFoldTableEntry &Entry : MemoryFoldTable4)
5633  // Index 4, folded load
5634  addTableEntry(Entry, TB_INDEX_4 | TB_FOLDED_LOAD);
5635 
5636  // Broadcast tables.
5637  for (const X86MemoryFoldTableEntry &Entry : BroadcastFoldTable2)
5638  // Index 2, folded broadcast
5639  addTableEntry(Entry, TB_INDEX_2 | TB_FOLDED_LOAD | TB_FOLDED_BCAST);
5640 
5641  for (const X86MemoryFoldTableEntry &Entry : BroadcastFoldTable3)
5642  // Index 2, folded broadcast
5643  addTableEntry(Entry, TB_INDEX_3 | TB_FOLDED_LOAD | TB_FOLDED_BCAST);
5644 
5645  // Sort the memory->reg unfold table.
5646  array_pod_sort(Table.begin(), Table.end());
5647 
5648  // Now that it's sorted, ensure its unique.
5649  assert(std::adjacent_find(Table.begin(), Table.end()) == Table.end() &&
5650  "Memory unfolding table is not unique!");
5651  }
5652 
5653  void addTableEntry(const X86MemoryFoldTableEntry &Entry,
5654  uint16_t ExtraFlags) {
5655  // NOTE: This swaps the KeyOp and DstOp in the table so we can sort it.
5656  if ((Entry.Flags & TB_NO_REVERSE) == 0)
5657  Table.push_back({Entry.DstOp, Entry.KeyOp,
5658  static_cast<uint16_t>(Entry.Flags | ExtraFlags) });
5659  }
5660 };
5661 }
5662 
5663 static ManagedStatic<X86MemUnfoldTable> MemUnfoldTable;
5664 
5665 const X86MemoryFoldTableEntry *
5666 llvm::lookupUnfoldTable(unsigned MemOp) {
5667  auto &Table = MemUnfoldTable->Table;
5668  auto I = llvm::lower_bound(Table, MemOp);
5669  if (I != Table.end() && I->KeyOp == MemOp)
5670  return &*I;
5671  return nullptr;
5672 }
